| classificacao         | enum('G','PG','PG-13','R','NC-17')                                  | YES  |     | G                 |                                        |
| recursos_especiais    | set('Trailers','Commentaries','Deleted Scenes','Behind the Scenes') | YES  |     | NULL              |                                        |
